25 /**
26  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
27  */
28 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
29                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
30                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
31                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
32                                 val userService: UserService,
33                                 eventService: EventService,
34                                 locationService: LocationService,
35                                 importService: ImportService)
36     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
37     extends AbstractController(cc)
38     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
39     with Util {
40 
41   val log = Logger("api.event")
42 
43   def getEvent(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
44     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
45 
46     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
47 
48     db.run(q.detailed).flatMap(x => x.headOption match {
49       case Some(r) => {
50         if (!r.location.latitude.isDefined || r.location.latitude == Some(0)) {
51           locationService.geocode(r.location).map(l => Ok(Json.toJson(r.copy(location = l))))
52         } else {
53           Future.successful(Ok(Json.toJson(r)))
54         }
55       }
56       case _ => Future.successful(NotFound)
57     })
58   }
59 
60   def getEventByShortId(id: String) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
61     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
62 
63     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.shortId === id) yield e;
64 
65     db.run(q.detailed).flatMap(x => x.headOption match {
66       case Some(r) => {
67         if (!r.location.latitude.isDefined || r.location.latitude == Some(0)) {
68           locationService.geocode(r.location).map(l => Ok(Json.toJson(r.copy(location = l))))
69         } else {
70           Future.successful(Ok(Json.toJson(r)))
71         }
72       }
73       case _ => Future.successful(NotFound)
74     })
75   }
76 
77   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Long], category: Option[Long],
78                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
79     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
80     
81     val q = for {
82       e <- event if upper(e.name) like upper(search.map(y => "%"++y++"%").getOrElse("%%").bind)
83                  /*if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""*/
84                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1l)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1l).bind === -1l
85                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1l).bind === 0l || location.getOrElse(-1l).bind === -1l
86                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
87                  if e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp
88     } yield e
89 
90 
91 
92     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
93     returnPaged(s,q,db)
94   }
95 
96   def getNearby(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
97     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
98 
99     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
100 
101     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
102       case Some(e) => {
103         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
104           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
105               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
106           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
107         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
108         returnPaged(s,q,db)
109       }
110       case None => Future(NotFound)
111     }
112   }
113 
114   def getSameViewed(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
115     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
116 
117     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
118       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
119       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
120       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
121 
122     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
123 
124     returnPaged(s,q,db)
125   }
126 
127   def deleteEvent(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
128     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
129 
130     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
131 
132     db.run(q).map {
133       case 0 => NotFound
134       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
135     }
136   }
137 
138   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
139     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
140       form => {
141         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
142       },
143       data => {
144         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
145 
146         eventService.insertEvent(data, organizer).map {
147           case Some(ev) => Ok(Json.toJson(ev))
148           case None => BadRequest
149         }
150       })
151   }
152 
153   def updateEvent(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
154     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
155       form => {
156         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
157       },
158       data => {
159         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
160 
161         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
162 
163         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
164 
165         val catParents = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
166             case cat =>
167               cat.id match {
168                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).flatMap(_.parent).result
169               }
170           }
171 
172         val catSimple = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
173             case cat =>
174               cat.id match {
175                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
176               }
177           }
178         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(catSimple ++ catParents).map(_.flatten.distinct)
179 
180         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
181 
182         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
183           case (((images,categories),Some(ev)),Some(location)) => {
184             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
185                               data.description,
186                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1l),
187                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax, ev.shortId)
188 
189             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
190 
191             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
192               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
193           }
194           case _ => Future.successful(None)
195         }.flatMap {
196           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
197             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
198             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
199             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
200 
201             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1l),event.id.getOrElse(-1l),EntityType.Event, img._2))
202             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1l),event.id.getOrElse(-1l)))
203             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1l)).detailed
204             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
205           }
206           case None => Future.successful(None)
207         }.map {
208           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
209           case None => BadRequest
210         }
211       })
212   }
213 
214   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
215     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
216 
217     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
218       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
219 
220       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
221      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
222   }
223 
224   def participate(id: Long) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
225     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
226 
227     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
228       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1l).bind).result)
229 
230     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
231       case (Some(e),None) => {
232         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1l),id)))
233         Future.successful(Ok)
234       }
235       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
236       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
237     }
238   }
239 
240   def unparticipate(id: Long) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
241     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
242 
243     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1l).bind).delete)
244       .flatMap {
245       case 1 => {
246         Future.successful(Ok)
247       }
248       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
249     }
250   }
251 
252   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
253     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
254 
255     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
256   }
257 
258   def importFacebookEvent(url: String) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
259     log.debug("Rest request to import event from url")
260 
261     importService.getEvent(url, request.identity)
262       .map(x => x.map(y => Ok(Json.toJson(y))).getOrElse(BadRequest))
263   }
264   
265   def copy(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
266     log.debug("Rest request to copy event")
267 
268     db.run(EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id && x.creatorId === organizer.id).detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
269       case Some(ev) => {
270         val locationForm = LocationForm.Data(ev.location.id, ev.location.name, ev.location.country,
271                                              ev.location.city, ev.location.street, ev.location.website,
272                                              ev.location.phone, ev.location.comment, ev.location.link, ev.location.zip)
273         val eventForm = EventForm.Data(ev.name, ev.from, ev.to, ev.categories.map(_.category), locationForm, 
274                                   ev.images.map(x => TaggedImageForm.Data(x.id.get, x.tag)), ev.description, ev.priceMin, ev.priceMax)
275         
276         eventService.insertEvent(eventForm, organizer).map {
277           case Some(event) => Ok(Json.toJson(event))
278           case _ => BadRequest
279         }
280       }
281       case None => Future.successful(BadRequest)
282     }
283   }
